 PROPOSAL 3: APPROVAL TO AMEND THE COMPANYвАЩS CHARTER TO, AT THE DISCRETION OF THE BOARD OF DIRECTORS, EFFECT A REVERSE STOCK SPLIT 
 
 
 Gene al 
 
 
 Ou Boa d app o ed and decla ed ad isable, subjec o s ockholde app o al, an amendmen o ou cha e which would e ec a e e se s ock spli ( he вАЬRe e se S ock Spli вАЭ) o ou issued common s ock by combining issued sha es o common s ock in o a lesse numbe o issued sha es o common s ock a a a io o no less han 1- o -5 and no mo e han 1- o -200, wi h he exac a io o be se wi hin his ange by ou Boa d a i s sole disc e ion. We belie e ha enabling ou Boa d o ix he speci ic a io o he Re e se S ock Spli wi hin he s a ed ange will p o ide us wi h he lexibili y o implemen he spli in a manne designed o maximize he an icipa ed bene i s o us and ou s ockholde s. The de e mina ion o he a io o he Re e se S ock Spli will be based on a numbe o ac o s as desc ibed below unde he heading вАЬDe e mina ion o he Re e se S ock Spli Ra io.вАЭ The o m o he p oposed ce i ica e o amendmen o ou cha e o e ec he Re e se S ock Spli is a ached as Appendix¬†B o his p oxy s a emen . 
 
 
 Reasons o he Re e se S ock Spli P oposal 
 

 
 Ou s ockholde base includes a signi ican numbe o e ail in es o s. As o June 5, 2025, e ail in es o s held app oxima ely 50% o ou ou s anding common s ock. The CompanyвАЩs expe ience o e he las ew¬†yea s is ha a signi ican numbe o i s e ail in es o s do no , ei he di ec ly o h ough hei b oke age accoun s, comple e hei p oxies o o he wise deli e o ing ins uc ions.  PROPOSAL 8: RATIFICATION OF APPOINTMENT OF INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTANTS 
 
 
 In oduc ion

As a ma e o good co po a e go e nance, he Audi Commi ee has de e mined o submi i s selec ion o s ockholde s o a i ica ion. I he selec ion o he independen audi o s is a i ied, he Audi Commi ee in i s disc e ion may selec di e en independen audi o s a any ime du ing he yea i i de e mines ha such a change would be in he bes in e es s o he Company and i s s ockholde s. 
 
 
 The Audi Commi ee has implemen ed p ocedu es unde he CompanyвАЩs Audi Commi ee p e-app o al policy o audi and non-audi se ices ( he вАЬP e-App o al PolicyвАЭ) o ensu e ha all audi and pe mi ed non-audi se ices o be p o ided o he Company ha e been p e-app o ed by he Audi Commi ee. Speci ically, he Audi Commi ee p e-app o es he use o Deloi e & Touche LLP o speci ic audi and non-audi se ices, wi hin app o ed mone a y limi s. I a p oposed se ice has no been p e-app o ed pu suan o he P e-App o al Policy, hen i mus be speci ically p e-app o ed by he Audi Commi ee be o e i may be p o ided by Deloi e & Touche LLP. Any p e- app o ed se ices exceeding he p e-app o ed mone a y limi s equi e speci ic app o al by he Audi Commi ee. Fo addi ional in o ma ion conce ning he Audi Commi ee and i s ac i i ies wi h Deloi e & Touche LLP, see вАЬCommi ees and Mee ings o he Boa d o Di ec o sвАЭ and вАЬAudi Commi ee Repo вАЭ abo e. 
 
 
 Rep esen a i es o Deloi e & Touche LLP a ended ou mee ings o he Audi Commi ee du ing 2024. We expec ha a ep esen a i e o Deloi e & Touche LLP will be p esen ia li e webcas a he Annual Mee ing and will ha e an oppo uni y o make a s a emen i he o she so desi es and o espond o app op ia e ques ions. 
 
 
 Vo e Requi ed o App o al 
 
 
 A quo um being p esen , he a i ma i e o e o he holde s o a majo i y o he o es p ope ly cas is equi ed o he a i ica ion o Deloi e & Touche LLP as he CompanyвАЩs independen egis e ed public accoun ing i m o 2025. Abs en ions and b oke non- o es will no ha e an e ec on he ou come o his P oposal 8. 
 
 
 Recommenda ion o he Boa d 
 
 
 THE BOARD OF DIRECTORS UNANIMOUSLY RECOMMENDS A VOTE вАЬFORвАЭ THE RATIFICATION OF DELOITTE & TOUCHE LLP AS THE COMPANYвАЩS INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM FOR 2025.

IF PROPERLY EXECUTED AND NO DIRECTION IS MADE, THIS PROXY WILL BE VOTED вАЬFORвАЭ THE DIRECTOR NOMINEES NAMED IN PROPOSAL 1, вАЬFORвАЭ THE APPROVAL OF AN AMENDMENT TO THE COMPANYвАЩS CHARTER TO INCREASE THE NUMBER OF AUTHORIZED SHARES OF THE COMPANYвАЩS COMMON STOCK FROM 1,500,000,000 SHARES TO 3,000,000,000 SHARES IN PROPOSAL 2, вАЬFORвАЭ THE APPROVAL OF AN AMENDMENT TO THE COMPANYвАЩS CHARTER TO, AT THE DISCRETION OF THE BOARD OF DIRECTORS, EFFECT A REVERSE STOCK SPLIT WITH RESPECT TO THE COMPANYвАЩS ISSUED COMMON STOCK, INCLUDING STOCK HELD BY THE COMPANY AS TREASURY SHARES, AT A RATIO OF NOT LESS THAN 1-FOR-5 AND NOT MORE THAN 1-FOR-200, WITH THE EXACT RATIO TO BE DETERMINED BY THE BOARD OF DIRECTORS IN PROPOSAL 3, вАЬFORвАЭ THE APPROVAL OF AN AMENDMENT TO THE COMPANYвАЩS CHARTER TO PROVIDE THAT THE AUTHORIZED NUMBER OF SHARES OF THE COMPANYвАЩS COMMON STOCK OR UNDESIGNATED PREFERRED STOCK MAY BE INCREASED OR DECREASED BY THE REQUISITE VOTE OF THE HOLDERS OF CAPITAL STOCK ENTITLED TO VOTE THEREON, WITHOUT EITHER CLASS VOTING AS A SEPARATE CLASS IRRESPECTIVE OF THE PROVISIONS OF SECTION 242(b)(2) OF THE DGCL IN PROPOSAL 4, вАЬFORвАЭ THE APPROVAL OF AN AMENDMENT TO THE COMPANYвАЩS CHARTER TO PROVIDE FOR EXCULPATION OF OFFICERS FROM BREACHES OF FIDUCIARY DUTY TO THE EXTENT PERMITTED BY THE DGCL IN PROPOSAL 5, вАЬFORвАЭ THE APPROVAL OF AN AMENDMENT TO THE COMPANYвАЩS 2021 PLAN TO INCREASE THE NUMBER OF SHARES OF THE COMPANYвАЩS COMMON STOCK RESERVED THEREUNDER BY 40,000,000 SHARES, FROM 51,400,000 SHARES TO 91,400,000 SHARES IN PROPOSAL 6, вАЬFORвАЭ THE APPROVAL OF THE NON-BINDING ADVISORY VOTE REGARDING THE COMPENSATION OF THE COMPANYвАЩS NAMED EXECUTIVE OFFICERS IN PROPOSAL 7, AND вАЬFORвАЭ THE RATIFICATION OF DELOITTE & TOUCHE LLP AS THE COMPANYвАЩS INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM FOR 2025 IN PROPOSAL 8. THIS PROXY WILL BE VOTED IN THE DISCRETION OF THE PROXIES ON ANY OTHER MATTERS THAT MAY PROPERLY COME BEFORE THE MEETING.
